"<p><strong><span>TODAY – IN THE ARCTIC</span></strong></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein</span></strong></p> 
 <p><span>Hello. I'm scientist Viktor Frankenstein, here in the Arctic trying to find a monster I've created. I've been having all this trouble with one monster. And to think that I was about to create another one! The Creature threatened me and my family if I didn't make it a bride. Well, it said it felt lonely. There I was on a Scottish island far away working on it: mixing chemicals, sewing flesh and bone together. Then I thought it was madness and destroyed it! But the monster saw me doing it through a window. It was angry! Yes, very angry!</span></p> 
 <p><span><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> – AT THE ORKNEY ISLANDS</strong></span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Creature<br /></span></strong><strong><span>How could you break</span><span> your promise? </span></strong><span>You have just destroyed my only hope of happiness! Do you think you'll get married and live happily with a wife while I am all alone and sad?</span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein<br /></span></strong><span>Go to hell, you horrible Creature!</span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Creature<br /></span></strong><span>I'll have my revenge. I'll be with you on your wedding night!</span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>TODAY – IN THE ARCTIC</span></strong></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein<br /></span></strong><span>The threat kept ringing in my ears. Was he going to kill me? Elizabeth would be very upset! A dead husband on her wedding night! These thoughts were going round and round in my head when I collected the body parts of what would be the Creature's bride and put them in a basket. I dragged the heavy basket to my boat and I left the island. I threw the basket into the sea. </span><span>All of a sudden I felt better. I thought I had done the right thing.</span><span>And I found myself thinking of my bright future with Elizabeth, my love, and my father, and my good friend Henry. &quot;He must be having fun at this very </span><span>moment&quot;, I thought. I really wanted to join him. But the strong winds took me to a small village on the Irish coast and something strange happened…</span></p> 
 <p><span><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> – SMALL FISHING VILLAGE IN IRELAND</strong></span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Policeman<br /></span></strong><span>What a crowd! Come on. Come on, let me through. Let me through. Go home! Aren't you fishermen? Go fishing! Let the police do their duty!</span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein<br /></span></strong><span>What's going on?</span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Policeman<br /></span></strong><span>You come with me, sir. You have to explain what happened to the man whose body we found. </span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein<br /></span></strong><span>A body? Whose body? </span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Policeman<br /></span></strong><span>A body was found on the beach. The man had been killed. A fisherman says he saw a boat with a single man in it at a short distance from the beach. That boat looked like yours… We'll take you to see the body, Sir.</span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>TODAY – IN THE ARCTIC</span></strong></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein</span></strong></p> 
 <p><span>And so they did. &quot;<strong>Who lost their life</strong></span><span>?&quot; It was Henry! My best friend was killed! I was very upset and I can't remember much of what happened next. I'm told I had to be </span><span>carriedout</span><span> of the morgue. I had a fever and started saying that I was the murderer of William, Justine and Henry. I was arrested. When they found a letter from home in my pocket, they got in touch with my father in Geneva. He came to help me until I was allowed to go back home. </span></p> 
 <p><span><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> – SMALL FISHING VILLAGE IN IRELAND</strong></span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Policeman<br /></span></strong><span>Well, Mr Alphonse Frankenstein, an important piece of information was brought to me. Your son was at the Orkney Islands at the hour the body of Mr Henry Clerval was found. Another fisherman saw him there. Take good care of this young man. He's been saying he's murdered someone called William, and Justine…</span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br /></span></strong><span>He's sick. But we'll get back to Geneva where Elizabeth, his bride, is waiting for him. He'll get better.</span></p> 
 <p><span><strong>TODAY – </strong><strong>IN THE ARCTIC</strong></span></p> 
 <p><strong><span>Viktor Frankenstein<br /></span></strong><span>My father was very happy but I was not. Henry was certainly killed by the monster and <strong>who knew where this nightmare would end</strong></span><span>? Sometimes I thought I should tell my father about the Creature, but he might think I was mad. </span><strong><span>Who'd believe a Creature can be brought back</span></strong><span> </span><strong><span>from the dead? </span></strong><span>Would you? Nobody knew my life was under threat. The Creature could be watching me… I'll tell you about my arrival to Geneva and my meeting with Elizabeth next time. Would we really get married or would the monster kill again? I was afraid, very afraid…</span></p>

"<p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hello. I'm scientist Viktor Frankenstein. You've been listening to the story the Creature told me long ago before I had to come after it and arrived here in the Arctic. The monster I built... I&nbsp;<strong>used to care&nbsp;</strong>about my science more than anything and I thought I could control nature. I've paid a high price for that. The Creature murdered my young brother and his nanny was executed for the crime. During that conversation years ago the monster told me he would go away and harm nobody else if I built him a bride. Should I do it? He wanted to have his answer when we sat by the fire in his hut in the mountains.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong>&nbsp;- IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, SITTING BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>So, what do you say? If you give me a bride you'll never see or hear from me again.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Alright. I'll do it.</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Will you?! That's great! Go home and start working. I'll watch your progress and when my bride is ready to come to life I'll be there.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY -&nbsp;</strong><strong>IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>For some reason I didn't want to start my work. I didn't want to do it in my father's house in Geneva, for sure. I didn't want him to find out about the monster. I was worried... and adding to that the monster had warned me he would watch me at a distance... My love, Elizabeth, noticed I wasn't happy.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong>&nbsp;- AT THE FRANKENSTEIN HOME IN GENEVA</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>You've been so quiet lately. We&nbsp;<strong>used to talk</strong>&nbsp;a lot. What's happening? Don't you like me anymore?</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Don't be silly! Of course I like you. I... I'll even keep the promise I made to my mother before she died, who was very fond of you. How about marriage? Will you marry me?</p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Marriage?! Mr Frankenstein, did you hear what your son Viktor has just said? He asked me to marry him!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>That's fantastic news! My late wife and I&nbsp;<strong>used to watch</strong>&nbsp;you both playing together as children and we thought you were made for each other. You'll make a wonderful couple!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Indeed, father. But first... well... I need to spend some time in England.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>England, my son?!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes, father... there are some new scientific discoveries there which I must see for myself. And, well... this could be my last chance to travel and see the world before I settle down. We can have our wedding as soon as I come back, my dear Elizabeth.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>We understand, son. But well... you'll need a good friend to take care of you, won't you? I'll ask Henry, your best friend, to go with you.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Henry?</p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes. That's a great idea. Henry loves travelling and will surely agree to go!</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY -&nbsp;</strong><strong>IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>My plan was to go to England and build a bride for the Creature. How could I keep my work a secret from Henry? We&nbsp;<strong>used to have</strong>&nbsp;fun travelling together but this time it was different. We stopped in many cities and when we reached Edinburgh I had to leave him behind...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong>&nbsp;- AT A RESTAURANT IN EDINBURGH</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>That's a great restaurant, don't you think so?<strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes. I suppose so.</p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>What's going on with you, Viktor? I'm not used to seeing you this sad. What's the problem?</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I think I need some time alone to think...</p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>To think?</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes. I need to think about my life. Let's make a deal: I'll go away for a month or two on my own and when I'm back everything will be what it&nbsp;<strong>used to be</strong>: we'll have a lot of fun together! I promise!</p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>OK. I'll be waiting for you.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY -&nbsp;</strong><strong>IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Well, I promised Henry a good time and the Creature a bride. I started collecting material and rented a hut far away in the Orkney Islands. But I had mixed feelings. It had been three years since I built the Creature and what a big mistake that was. What if the monsters didn't like each other? And if the female creature started killing people too? And... and if... if they had babies and there were hundreds of monsters!I couldn't allow this to happen! It was too dangerous. I hadn't finished the work yet but I couldn't give life to another monster. So I just destroyed it! It was over! No more bride. But what about the Creature? Was I going to pay a heavy price for destroying the female monster - the friend the monster was expecting to be happy with? I'll tell you next time.&nbsp;</p>

"<p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, SITTING BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hello, I'm the Creature. And I've been telling you and my creator, Viktor Frankenstein, about my experience meeting people. Some feared me, some hated me and finally I found a man who was kind to me... Well, he was blind and couldn't see my ugly face. But I hoped he might help me persuade others I'm good and loving... There I was, in his house, when his children arrived. What would they do when they saw me?</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> - IN THE DELACEYS' HOME</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Girl<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh! What is that? Ohhhhhh...</p> 
 <p><strong>Boy<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Sister? She's <strong>fainted</strong>! Get away from my father you monster! Don't be frightened, Dad! Get out of here, ugly monster! This will show you!</p>

 <p><strong>Boy<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Out! Out!</p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Son, what's going on?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Ouch! Arrrrrgh!</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh that boy beat me with a stick! And he beat me and beat me! I could have killed him but... I just ran away. I was really angry! I wanted to be their best friend... But it was not going to happen. That's when I decided life is a war against man! Then I thought <strong>you, Dr Frankenstein, might be the only person </strong>to give me some answers. You, my creator!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>How did you know where I lived?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Papers I took from your laboratory in Germany said you came from Geneva and that's where I was going! It took me two months to reach the place. One night I was ready to go to sleep when I heard the voice of a child...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> - IN THE WOODS NEAR GENEVA</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>William<br clear=""none"" /></strong>(Humming a song)</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>The beautiful boy looked innocent and I thought <strong>he might accept</strong> my appearance. I decided that I would take him with me to be my friend. I wouldn't be lonely anymore. But when I caught him... well, I tried to tell him I wouldn't harm him.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> - IN THE WOODS NEAR GENEVA</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>William<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Let me go, horrible monster! Let me go or I'll tell my daddy! He's a powerful man! He'll beat you! His name is Frankenstein!</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>That name <strong>took me by surprise</strong>! The name of my enemy! I felt so much hate... I put my hands around his neck and I held it. Yes, I held it tight and... suddenly I realised he went silent.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>My brother William! My father is called Alphonse. Alphonse Frankenstein. And he doesn't even know about you!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I knew this would make you suffer! You made me suffer and now I realised <strong>I could make you suffer too</strong>.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>And what happened to Justine, William's nanny, who was executed as his murderer?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I found this lovely woman sleeping in a hut. I thought about waking her up but... I was sure she wouldn't be nice to me! She should suffer for that!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>And what did you do?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I put a locket with the picture of a woman I took from the boy's body in her pocket. My life is very sad and I made her pay for it!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Horrible creature! You're responsible for the deaths of two good and innocent people!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I told you, I was good too. But now I'm sad and alone! Nobody will ever love me... unless you create a woman - a monster like me - whom I can share my life with.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Another monster like you? No!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>What I ask you is fair. If you give me another creature that looks like me, <strong>I could go </strong>and take it far away to South America. I'll make sure nobody will ever see us again.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>No more contact with people?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>No. Never again.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Let me think about it. I'll tell you my decision next time.</p>

"<p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, SITTING BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hello, I'm... Viktor Frankenstein's Creature. Here we are, in my hut on the mountains. I'm happy to tell you and Viktor Frankenstein my story. How I learnt about the day, the night, the hunger, thirst, cold... And I learnt how to live with all this the hard way. Imagine that I tried to touch fire?! How silly of me. Of course I was burnt. But I saw good things too. These little creatures <strong>which made pleasant sounds</strong>. Yes, the birds. I tried to sound like them but nothing came out of my mouth! And I saw people. I've never learnt how to behave with you humans. I was surprised when people <strong>who saw me ran away</strong>. In the villages, some men wanted to hurt me.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> - IN THE VILLAGE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Vigilante 1<br clear=""none"" /></strong>So do you all have things you can use as weapons with you?</p> 
 <p><strong>Crowd<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes!</p> 
 <p><strong>Boy<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I have a few stones <strong>that I can throw at the monster</strong>. I'm a good shot!</p> 
 <p><strong>Vigilante 1<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Go home, boy. The monster could be dangerous. It was seen trying to get into the house near the central square.</p> 
 <p><strong>Vigilante 2<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Shall we go and look for it? This time we might get lucky, catch it and kill it!</p> 
 <p><strong>Crowd<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Kill it! Kill the monster!</p> 
 <p><strong>Vigilante 1<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Let's go then. We can start near the vegetable garden <strong>where he was seen last time</strong>... Let's go!</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>All these people seemed angry with me... Why?I escaped to the open country and hid in a hut. That was where I was when I watched a family in a nearby house. I heard they were called the De Laceys. I was careful not to allow them to see me. The boy, the girl and an old man looked poor but happy...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> - IN THE DE LACEYS' HOME</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Girl<br clear=""none"" /></strong>That's what we have for dinner today. Some carrots, potatoes, cheese, bread... just one egg. You like eggs, dad. This one is for you.</p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>You're very generous, dear daughter. But you should have this egg.</p> 
 <p><strong>Girl<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Maybe we should give it to my brother then. He's been working hard and he needs more food.</p> 
 <p><strong>Boy<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Thank you, sister. I'll try to work harder so that we can have more eggs to eat.</p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I'm very grateful, son. A blind man's life isn't easy... The light in my life is the love of my children.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>They were so kind to one another... I wanted to be part of their family. I learned to speak by listening to them in hiding. I discovered books lost in the forest and learned how to read. And at that time I finally found out why people ran away from me. I saw my own face in a pond and... I'm really ugly! I didn't want to frighten this family. I had to find a way to talk to them. I thought about the father. He was blind and so he wouldn't see me. One day, using all my courage, I knocked at the door...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST</strong><strong> - IN THE DELACEYS' HOME</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Who's there? Come in.</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Please excuse me, Sir. I've been travelling and I was wondering if I could rest here for a while.<strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Sure. I can't see and my children, <strong>who take care of me</strong>, are not here at the moment, or I'd offer you some food.</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Do not worry yourself, kind man. I'm looking for some friends and I fear these good people won't accept me.</p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>That's sad. But if these friends are good people, can't you persuade them to accept you?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I plan to start doing it now. But they believe that I want to harm them…</p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>You sound honest. I can try and help you. Who are your friends?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh, Sir. You are the first person <strong>who has been kind to me</strong>!&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>BROTHER AND SISTER COME INTO THEIR HOME</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Just a minute... I can hear my children coming.&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh, no! They'll see me! Please, take care of me good man! You and your family are the friends I want!</p> 
 <p><strong>Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Are we? Who are you?</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE CREATURE'S HUT, BY THE FIRE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>The door opened and there they were - the old man's two children. Did they kiss me? Did they run away? That's what I'm going to tell you next time.</p> 
 "
"<p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hello. I'm Viktor Frankenstein. I've been telling you about how my young brother was murdered and his nanny was executed for the crime. But she was innocent! I felt guilty because I think the boy was killed by my creature. Yes, I've created the most evil creature on Earth! Nobody knew about it. I was so sad and lonely. I missed those days when I didn't worry so much. One morning I decided to go alone to the top of Montavert, where I had an unexpected meeting...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - ON TOP OF THE MOUNTAIN</strong><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh... this was a steep climb. But I finally reached the top... Oh, what a view! It's fantastic! The air is so fresh!&nbsp;<strong>I feel so much better now!</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>A NOISE IN THE BUSHES</strong><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Who's there?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh... Here I am.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>It's you, monster!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I came to talk to you.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I hate you! Don't you fear I might hurt you? Go away! If you stay here I'll kill you! I wish I could bring back the people you killed just by... just by killing you!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I expected this welcome. Everybody hates me.&nbsp;<strong>You, my creator, hate me the most</strong>. But if you do your duty towards me, I'll do mine towards you and all the other people - all men and women.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Duty?!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes. I'll leave everybody in peace if you do one thing for me; but if you refuse, I'll kill your friends and family.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Horrible monster! I will kill you first!</p> 
 <p><strong>FRANKENSTEIN TRIES TO ATTACK THE CREATURE</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Running from me, you coward? Come here. I'm gonna catch you!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Be calm! Haven't I suffered enough? My life is difficult but it's important to me and I'll fight for it.&nbsp;<strong>Remember that I am stronger than you</strong>.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Well, I have to admit that you are.</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh Frankenstein, don't be like all the others who are hostile to me.&nbsp;<strong>Remember, that I'm your creature, and at the moment, the saddest creature of all</strong>. I see people happy everywhere. I feel rejected. I'm very lonely.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Because you are disgusting!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>It's not my fault. I was good and had a kind heart; suffering made me bad. Make me happy, and I'll be good again.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>What do you want me to do?</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Follow me and hear my story.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>He led the way and I followed him. I kept thinking about what he had just said... Well... he had a point. I had created him. I was feeling sorry for him but I was also curious and... and wanted to know if he had really killed my brother. Maybe he didn't. We went into a hut. I sat by the fire to listen to his story. He looked happy to see me there.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - IN THE CREATURE'S HUT</strong>&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Well.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Well, here we are.</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>It's difficult for me to remember my first moments. I was so confused. Light hurt my eyes and I realised it was the sun. I was hungry and thirsty...</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes, the Creature was like a child when I left it all alone in my laboratory. I ran away in fear when it woke up. Maybe I had a duty towards it. The Creature was left to find its way in the world for itself. It learnt how to survive in the forest, and... it had its first contact with man. How did it go? I'll let the Creature itself tell you all about it. That's what you'll hear next time...</p>

"<p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hello, I'm scientist Viktor Frankenstein – well, I used to be a scientist but I came to hate everything about my job. I was back in the town where I was born, Geneva, after six years at university in Germany. I was brought back by bad news in my father's letter. I found him, and my sweet Elizabeth, very upset. My young brother William had been killed! How? By whom? The police were there too.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - AT THE FRANKENSTEIN FAMILY HOME</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Policeman<br clear=""none"" /></strong>We're doing everything we can to find who killed your son, Mr Alphonse Frankenstein.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Thank you, detective.</p> 
 <p><strong>Policeman<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Miss Elizabeth, we're sorry about what happened to the boy: we know you're very close to the family.</p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes.</p> 
 <p><strong>Policeman<br clear=""none"" /></strong>The marks of the killer's fingers that we found on the boy's neck were still fresh. The body was in the woods.</p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>That's horrible!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Calm down, my dear Elizabeth. Sir, we were having a family day out and my son William disappeared.</p> 
 <p><strong>Policeman<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Very unfortunate, Mr Frankenstein. But<strong>&nbsp;we've just arrested&nbsp;</strong>a suspect.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>A suspect?! Who killed my boy?</p> 
 <p><strong>Policeman<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Well, we found a valuable locket with the boy's mother's picture in the pocket of one of the nanny's dresses.</p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Justine?! It's not possible!</p> 
 <p><strong>Policeman<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I'm sorry, Miss Elizabeth.&nbsp;<strong>Justine hasn't explained yet&nbsp;</strong>how it got there! Was it stolen?</p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>But I know she's innocent!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Elizabeth my dear, I want to believe that she's innocent, but what about the locket?</p> 
 <p><strong>Elizabeth<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Everyone believes Justine is guilty. I don't. She loved William very much.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes, everyone believed Justine had killed William - everyone except Elizabeth and I. Why? Because I knew who the murderer was. On my journey back to Geneva, I saw a very large figure run over the hills and disappear. It was the Creature! It was the murderer! And now, what would happen to poor Justine? She went to trial.</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - IN THE COURTROOM</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Prosecutor<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Justine, you were out the whole night in which the child was killed, weren't you?</p> 
 <p><strong>Justine<br clear=""none"" /></strong><strong>I've already told&nbsp;</strong>the police and everybody else. I paid a visit to my auntie in the village. On my way back I heard people talking about a boy who went missing. It was William. I spent hours looking for him.</p> 
 <p><strong>Prosecutor<br clear=""none"" /></strong>A woman from the market saw you near the place where the child's body was found. What were you doing there?</p> 
 <p><strong>Justine<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I didn't know I was near the place.</p> 
 <p><strong>Prosecutor<br clear=""none"" /></strong>The woman asked you what you were doing there. She said you sounded confused.</p> 
 <p><strong>Justine<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes. I was tired and worried about William.</p> 
 <p><strong>Prosecutor<br clear=""none"" /></strong>You went back to the Frankenstein family home in the morning and asked to be told any news about the boy.</p> 
 <p><strong>Justine<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes!&nbsp;<strong>I've just told</strong>&nbsp;you, I was worried about him!</p> 
 <p><strong>Prosecutor<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Or maybe you felt guilty... When shown the body you started to scream!</p> 
 <p><strong>Justine<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes. It was horrible! Horrible!</p> 
 <p><strong>Prosecutor<br clear=""none"" /></strong>And you stayed in your bed for several days. That's when someone found this: the boy's locket with a picture of his mother - yes, this very locket - in your dress pocket. How do you explain that?</p> 
 <p><strong>Justine<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I... I... I can't explain!</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Poor Justine! But I knew the monster had done something to make her look guilty... Our family was very rich and powerful. The crime was shocking. They had to find someone to blame quickly...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - IN THE COURTROOM</strong><strong><br /></strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Judge<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Silence! For the murder of the child William Frankenstein on May, the 7th, I sentence Justine Moritz to death!</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Justine was innocent but she was executed anyway. I felt that I was guilty of two deaths because I had created the monster! I couldn't eat. I couldn't sleep. So I decided to take long walks in the mountains. That's when I had an unexpected meeting. I'm going to tell you all about it next time.</p>

"<p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hello, I'm scientist Viktor Frankenstein. I've just been rescued here in the Arctic Circle. I feel weak but I have to continue my story and warn all of you about the dangers of science. At university in Germany all I wanted to do was to try and create life. I studied anatomy in my laboratory and spent days and nights in morgues and cemeteries collecting body parts...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - IN THE CEMETERY</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Guard<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hi there! I'm the night guard 'ere. This is my cemetery. Who are you?</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Who, me?</p> 
 <p><strong>Guard<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yeah... If I ask the others 'round 'ere they aren't going to answer, are they? They're in their coffins, being eaten up by the little worms.&nbsp;<strong>They've been worm supper for a long time!</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>The worms. Eyes, brain, so wonderful, so perfect, being eaten by worms...</p> 
 <p><strong>Guard<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Well, they're doing their business down there alright, but what business do you have 'ere? And what's this big bag you're carrying?</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh... nothing... these are my things... my scientific... I'm leaving now...</p> 
 <p><strong>Guard<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Don't come back 'ere! What does he want with dead people? The dead are dead and that's the end of it, I say.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Stupid man! Or was I the stupid one, the selfish one? I collected bones and flesh. I used bigger pieces because they were easier to work on and made me go faster. The creature was about 2.4 metres tall. It was ready on that rainy night in November...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - AT DR VIKTOR FRANKENSTEIN'S LABORATORY</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>It's all here now. Finally! Finally!&nbsp;<strong>I've waited for this moment for a long time</strong>. Actually,<strong>&nbsp;I've worked on this since I came to Germany two years ago</strong>. Oh... let me check these wires... they go to the roof... I'll use electricity. Yes, that Italian scientist, Galvani... that article I read... he made a dead frog jump using the power of electricity, but I, Viktor Frankenstein, will make a man rise from the dead!</p> 
 <p><strong>A CLAP OF THUNDER</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>(roaring)</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh... the arms are moving... the legs... the eyes are open... oh these yellow eyes... they are...</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>(roaring)</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>... they are... they are horrible! The skin is very pale... you can see through it. His hair is dark and his teeth are white, but his eyes are yellow and these black lips! What a horrible creature! I've created a monster!!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>(roaring)</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>No! No! Keep away from me, horrible creature!! I must escape!</p> 
 <p><strong>Creature<br clear=""none"" /></strong>(roaring)</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I ran! Oh how I ran! I spent the rest of the night walking in the rain. Then, in the morning, I heard a voice I recognised...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - IN THE STREETS OF INGOLSTADT</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hey Viktor! Viktor!&nbsp;<strong>I haven't seen you for so long</strong>! Don't you recognise me anymore? It's Henry!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Henry? Oh, of course, my dear friend! I didn't expect to see you here!</p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Good Lord, you look terrible! So thin and pale! It's good I'm here now. Your family back in Geneva is very worried.&nbsp;<strong>They haven't heard from you for a while</strong>.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes, I... I've been busy...</p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Never fear, Henry is here! I'm taking you home.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Home?!</p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes, your home, here in Germany, where you study.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>But... the monster...</p> 
 <p><strong>Henry<br clear=""none"" /></strong>What?</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Oh, nothing.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I didn't want to tell him about the Creature. But what if it was still there? Well, it wasn't after all. But I knew what I had done and I was worried. I felt ill. I had a fever. Henry took care of me. Things were going back to normal when a letter from my father brought terrible news. I had to go back to Geneva immediately. That's what I'm going to tell you next.</p>

"<p><strong>TODAY - IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Hello I'm Viktor Frankenstein. I'm a scientist from Switzerland. You might ask how I arrived here, in the Arctic Circle. Yes, it's far from home. I came this far upon the ice. But it's very cold and I almost died. I was rescued by an explorer's boat. Captain Walton is a kind man but he's... He's ready to do anything to push the limits of science. He's a fool! And so are you if you try to fight Nature! Pardon me... I'm sick. It's freezing here. But I had to come and find the monster I've created! Did I ever think I would feel this way about a Creature I gave life to? No, I did not! Never!&nbsp;<strong>I created life and all my Creature has ever caused is death!&nbsp;</strong>How did I give life to the Creature? My love of science started early. I remember one morning when I was on holiday in France with my father...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST - IN A FRENCH HOTEL</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein (13 years old)<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Look dad! Look!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Reading a book? That's good my boy. It's been raining for hours. Staying indoors isn't good for a thirteen year old but it's lucky - you found an interesting book here at the hotel.</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein (13 years old)<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Yes. I'm not bored anymore.&nbsp;<strong>Actually, I've never read anything so good</strong>. This book is fantastic!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein's Father<br clear=""none"" /></strong>What's it about? Let me see... Cornelius Agrippa! Oh, my dear Viktor, don't waste your time with this book. It's full of foolish ideas. Find another one.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY&nbsp;- IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I had in my hands a book by an alchemist who lived in the 1500s. My father didn't explain to me that Agrippa's ideas were old and had no place in modern science. So I went on to read books by other alchemists. I thought about the power of magic all the time. I wanted to find the elixir of life! Could I ever end diseases and control death? These were my thoughts when I went to the University of Ingolstadt, in Germany. But when I arrived there I didn't expect my professors to laugh at me.<em>&nbsp;</em></p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST -&nbsp;AT UNIVERSITY</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Professor&nbsp;</strong><strong>Krempe<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Have you really wasted your time studying these foolish ideas, young Frankenstein? Good God!</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein (17 years old)<br clear=""none"" /></strong>But Professor Krempe... I...</p> 
 <p><strong>Professor Krempe<br clear=""none"" /></strong><strong>Has n</strong><strong>obody ever told you these ideas are old and silly?</strong>&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein (17 years old)<br clear=""none"" /></strong>Well, no...&nbsp;<strong>It's never been explained to me why</strong>. I... I...&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>Professor&nbsp;</strong><strong>Krempe<br clear=""none"" /></strong>All is not lost, my dear sir. You must start again and study real science!&nbsp;<strong>&nbsp;</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY&nbsp;- IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I didn't like Professor Krempe at all! And modern science wasn't as exciting to me as the science of the old alchemists. Those men wanted to discover things about power and how to live forever. Perhaps their ideas didn't work but they were fantastic! I was disappointed... but not for long. What got me excited again was one particular class. Professor Waldman didn't laugh at the old alchemists I loved so much. I felt he understood me. Later I paid him a visit. He opened my eyes to other subjects. I remember his words well...</p> 
 <p><strong>IN THE PAST -&nbsp;AT UNIVERSITY</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Professor&nbsp;</strong><strong>Waldman<br clear=""none"" /></strong>If your wish is to become a real man of science, you must study everything, including chemistry and mathematics.</p> 
 <p><strong>TODAY&nbsp;- IN THE ARCTIC</strong></p> 
 <p><strong>Viktor Frankenstein<br clear=""none"" /></strong>I built my own laboratory in the room at the top of my house. And I studied hard. At the end of two years I even made some discoveries in chemistry. The other professors at the university were pleased. My father wrote me letters. He sent news about my young brothers and my childhood love Elizabeth but... I didn't give them much thought. I started to study anatomy and all I could think about was creating life! And I succeeded - unfortunately! And I'll tell you about how I gave life to the Creature next time.</p>

"<p><strong>Peter<br /></strong>It's quiet tonight.</p> 
 <p><strong>Mary<br /></strong>I know. It's a bit of a worry - Ceilia said tonight was our<strong>&nbsp;last hope</strong>. If we don't get any customers we might have to close.</p> 
 <p><strong>Gordon<br /></strong>Well,&nbsp;<strong>don't get your hopes up</strong>. This place has been&nbsp;<strong>on its knees</strong>&nbsp;ever since it opened. We've all had a laugh but I need to get a job at a proper restaurant, where the customers are queuing up to eat my food.</p> 
 <p><strong>Mary<br /></strong>Don't<strong>&nbsp;pin your hopes on it</strong>. It was your cooking that scared the customers away anyway. Hang on, did I just hear somebody come in?</p> 
 <p><strong>Peter<br /></strong>I'll go and check.</p> 
 <p><strong>Gordon</strong><br /><strong>To be honest</strong>, I might be able to take you with me, to my new job - but Peter - not a chance.</p> 
 <p><strong>Mary<br /></strong>I can only&nbsp;<strong>live in hope</strong>!</p> 
 <p><strong>Peter<br /></strong>Yes, we've got two customers! And they want... a cheese and tomato pizza. Can we do pizzas?</p> 
 <p><strong>Gordon</strong><br />Can we do pizzas?&nbsp;<strong>Not a hope in hell!&nbsp;</strong>Do I look like a chef who cooks 'pizzas'?!</p>

 <p><strong>Gordon<br /></strong>Yes... well... it's just a little bit beneath me... but I suppose I can give it a go.</p> 
 <p><strong>Mary</strong><br />Good. I'll tell Ceilia the good news.&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>Gordon</strong><br />Peter. Here's &pound;10 - run to the supermarket and buy some frozen pizzas. But shhh, it's our little secret.</p>

 <p><strong>Ceilia<br /></strong>Mmmm, something smells good. Great news about getting all the customers in - even though they only like pizza! It seems like there's&nbsp;<strong>a glimmer of hope</strong>&nbsp;for the business.</p> 
 <p><strong>Ceilia</strong><br />Looking good. Maybe pizzas are our future?&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>Peter<br /></strong>Yes, they're not bad for frozen pizzas are they?</p>

 <p><strong>Gordon<br /></strong>But what am I going to do? I can't just get a new job just like that.</p> 
 <p><strong>Ceilia<br /></strong>There might not be hope for you but I think I might have the perfect answer.</p> 
 <p><strong>LATER...</strong></p>

 <p><strong>Ceilia</strong><br />It must be the bake-off competition - always makes an effort when there's something to win! The first prize is &pound;500.</p> 
 <p><strong>Mary<br /></strong>Hi Gordon. Fantastic cake.</p> 
 <p><strong>Gordon<br /></strong>Cake? What cake?</p> 
 <p><strong>Mary<br /></strong>This one. Did you make it for the competition?</p> 
 <p><strong>Ceilia<br /></strong>The bake-off. The first prize is &pound;500.</p>

"<p><strong>Ceilia/Gordon/Mary&nbsp;<br /></strong>5... 4... 3... 2... 1...</p> 
 <p><strong>Gordon<br /></strong>That's it! It is exactly one week since The White Elephant opened and still not one…&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> 
 <p><strong>Peter<br /></strong>...customer!&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

 <p><strong>Ceilia</strong><br />Gordon, Gordon&nbsp;<strong>keep your hair on</strong>! Customer's is always right – and thank goodness we've got one.&nbsp;So, let's try to keep him happy and - who knows - he might bring his friends next time.</p>
